SELECT r1."Id", r1."Username", r1."Email", r0."Name" AS "Role", r1."Designation", d."Name" AS "Department", CASE r1."Status"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Approved'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Rejected'
    ELSE r1."Status"::text
END AS "Status", r1."CreatedAt"
FROM (
    SELECT r."Id", r."CreatedAt", r."DepartmentId", r."Designation", r."Email", r."RoleId", r."Status", r."Username"
    FROM "RegistrationRequests" AS r
    WHERE r."Status" = 0
    ORDER BY r."CreatedAt" DESC

) AS r1

SELECT i."Id" AS id, i."Name" AS name, c."Name" AS category, CASE
    WHEN i0."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN i0."AvailableQuantity"
    ELSE 0
END AS "availableQuantity", CASE
    WHEN i0."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN i0."TotalQuantity"
    ELSE 0
END AS "totalQuantity", i."Description" AS description
FROM "Items" AS i
INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON i."CategoryId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "InventoryStocks" AS i0 ON i."Id" = i0."ItemId"
